Setting up the grid

step 1

0.5"

Set	your	margins	based	upon	the	document	size		
you	are	building.

For	this	8.5"	x	11"	example,	the	image	margin	is	
0.25"	inches	and	the	text	margin	is	0.5"	inches.

step 2

Create	10	columns	within	the	text	margin,	and	set	
the	gutter	width	to	0.2"	inches.	Use	this	ratio	of	
margins	to	gutter	size	(1	:	4)	to	determine	gutter	
sizes	for	printed	communications	larger	than

The Pfizer dotted illustration style

Pfizer dotted illustration style
The	subject	matter	captured	by	the	illustrations	brings	the	concepts	within		
Our	Path	Forward	to	life.	The	illustrations	are	divided	into	themes	that	elevate	and		
support	messaging	to	help	tell	an	overall	story.	The	dotted	illustration	style	conveys		
the	aspirational	qualities	within	Pfizer’s	purpose	and	mission.

### 2018

**Logo Information:**

- Details on proper logo usage, including preferred gradient, reverse versions, alternate color options, minimum size, and clear-space rules.
- The preferred gradient version of the logo uses Cyan and PMS Reflex Blue. Minimum sizes: 0.3125 inches for the primary logo and 0.1875 inches for alternate logos.
- Do not outline, crop, rotate, or add shadows to the logo. Several other misuses such as misproportioned, placed in a holding box, or altered letterforms are listed.

**Color Information:**

- Primary, neutral, and secondary color palettes with Pantone, CMYK, RGB, and HEX details for Pfizer Blue and other supportive colors.
- Pfizer's primary color: Pfizer Blue (#0093D0), other colors include Cyan (#00AEEF), Yellow (#F7D417), Red (#CC292B), etc. Gradients are not allowed.

**Typography Information:**

- Pfizer's typography usage guidelines go here (details can be expanded on more extensive extraction).

**Imagery Photography:**

- Guidelines for placing the logo on various backgrounds and displays. Must ensure good contrast and maintain clear space to guarantee legibility.

**Spacing Layout:**

- Page discusses alignment and clear space rules (details to resolve later). Generally, logos require careful margin adherence.

**Notes:**

- The brand team is the point of contact for questions on guidelines. Resources are available via id.pfizer.com.

### Color Analysis
*Statistics computed across 478 images*

| Color | Mean |
|-------|------|
| White | 42.7% |
| Dark Blue | 29.2% |
| Light Blue | 28.1% |
| Gray | 21.7% |
| Black | 20.9% |
| Mud Green | 19.6% |
| Cyan | 18.2% |
| Dark Brown | 17.9% |

| Tone | Mean |
|------|------|
| Warm | 6.5% |
| Neutral | 60.4% |
| Cool | 33.1% |
